   BhG 9.1	Bhu 9.1
   śrī-bhagavān uvāca	SrI--BagavAn uvAca
   idaṃ tu te guhyatamaṃ pravakṣyāmy anasūyave |	idam tu te guhyatamam pravakzyAmi anasUyave |
   jñānaṃ vijñāna-sahitaṃ yaj jñātvā mokṣyase 'śubhāt ||1||	jQAnam vijQAna--sahitam yat jQAtvA mokzyase aSuBAt ||1||
   śrīdharaḥ -	SrIDaraH -
   pareśaḥ prāpyate śuddha-bhaktyeti sthitam aṣṭame |	para-ISaH prApyate SudDa-BaktyA-iti sTitam azwame |
   navame tu tad-aiśvaryam atyāścaryaṃ prapañcyate ||	navame tu tat--ESvaryam ati-AScaryam prapaQcyate ||
   evaṃ tāvat saptamāṣṭamayoḥ svīyaṃ pārameśvaraṃ tattvaṃ bhaktyaiva sulabhaṃ	evam tAvat saptama-azwamayoH svIyam pArameSvaram tattvam BaktyA-eva sulaBam
   nānyathā ity uktvā idānīm acintyaṃ svakīyam aiśvaryaṃ bhakteś cāsādhāraṇaṃ	na-anyaTA iti uktvA idAnIm acintyam svakIyam ESvaryam BakteH ca-asADAraNam
   prabhāva`aprapañcayiṣyan bhagavān uvāca idam iti | viśeṣeṇa jñāyate	praBAva`aprapaQcayizyan BagavAn uvAca idam iti | viSezeNa jQAyate
   'neneti vijñānam upāsanam | tat-sahitaṃ jñānam īśvara-viṣayam | idaṃ tv	anena-iti vijQAnam upAsanam | tat--sahitam jQAnam ISvara--vizayam | idam tu-
   anusūyave punaḥ punaḥ sva-māhātmyam evopadiśatīty evaṃ parama-kāruṇike	anusUyave punar punar sva-mAhAtmyam eva-upadiSati-iti evam parama-kAruNike
   mayi doṣa-dṛṣṭi-rahitāya | tubhyaṃ vakṣyāmi | tu-śabdo vaiśiṣṭye ||1||	mayi doza-dRzwi--rahitAya | tuByam vakzyAmi | tu-SabdaH vESizwye ||1||
   madhusūdanaḥ - pūrvādhyāye mūrdhany anāḍī-dvārakeṇa	maDusUdanaH  pUrva-aDyAye mUrDani anAxI-dvArakeNa
   hṛdaya-kaṇṭha-bhrū-madhyādi-dhāraṇā-sahitena	hRdaya--kaNWa--BrU--maDya-Adi-DAraNA--sahitena

   svecchayotkrānta-prāṇasyārcir-ādi-mārgeṇa brahma-lokaṃ prayātasya tatra	sva-icCayA-utkrAnta--prANasya-arciH--Adi--mArgeNa brahma-lokam prayAtasya tatra
   samyag-jñānodayena kalpānte para-brahma-prāpti-lakṣaṇā krama-muktir	samyak--jQAna-udayena kalpa-ante para--brahma--prApti-lakzaNA krama-muktiH-
   vyākhyātā | tatra cānenaiva prakāreṇa muktir labhyate nānayathety āśaṅkya-	vyAKyAtA | tatra ca-anena-eva prakAreNa muktiH laByate na-anayaTA-iti ASaFkya-
   ananya-cetāḥ satataṃ yo māṃ smarati nityaśaḥ | tasyāhaṃ sulabhaḥ ity ādinā	ananya--cetAH satatam yaH mAm smarati nityaSas | tasya-aham sulaBaH iti AdinA
   bhagavat-tattva-vijñānāt sākṣān mokṣa-prāptir abhihitā | tatra cānanyā	Bagavat--tattva--vijQAnAt sAkzAt mokza--prAptiH aBihitA | tatra ca-ananyA
   bhaktir asādhāraṇo hetur ity uktaṃ puruṣaḥ sa paraḥ pārtha bhaktyā labhyas	BaktiH asADAraNaH hetuH iti uktam puruzaH sa paraH pArTa BaktyA laByas
   tv ananyayā iti | tatra	tu ananyayA iti | tatra
   pūrvokta-yoga-dhāraṇā-pūrva-prāṇotkramaṇārcir-ādi-mārga-gamana-kāla-vilambādi-kleśam	pUrva-ukta--yoga--DAraNA--pUrva--prANa-utkramaNa-arciH--Adi--mArga--gamana--kAla--vilamba-Adi--kleSam
   antareṇaiva sākṣān mokṣa-prāptaye bhagavat-tattvasya tad-bhakteś ca	antareNa-eva sAkzAt mokza--prAptaye Bagavat--tattvasya tad--BakteH ca
   vistareṇa jñāpanāya navamo 'dhyāya ārabhyate | aṣṭame	vistareNa jQApanAya navamaH aDyAyaH AraByate | azwame
   dhyeya-brahma-nirūpaṇena tad-dhyāna-niṣṭhasya gatir uktā | navame tu	Dyeya--brahma--nirUpaNena tad--DyAna--nizWasya gatiH uktA | navame tu
   jñeya-brahma-nirūpaṇena jñāna-niṣṭhasya gatir ucyata iti saṅkṣepaḥ | tatra	jQeya--brahma--nirUpaNena jQAna--nizWasya gatiH ucyate iti saFkzepaH | tatra
   vakṣyamāṇa-jñāna-stuty-arthās trīn ślokān |	vakzyamANa--jQAna-stuty-arTAH trIn SlokAn |
   idaṃ prāg bahudhoktam agre ca vakṣyamāṇam adhunocyamānaṃ jñānaṃ	idam prAk bahuDA-uktam agre ca vakzyamANam aDunA-ucyamAnam jQAnam
   śabda-pramāṇakaṃ brahma-tattva-viṣayakaṃ te tubhyaṃ pravakṣyāmi |	Sabda-pramANakam brahma--tattva--vizayakam te tuByam pravakzyAmi |
   tu-śabdaḥ pūrvādhyāyoktād dhyānāj jñānasya vailakṣaṇyam āha | idam eva	tu-SabdaH pUrva-aDyAya-uktAt DyAnAt jQAnasya vElakzaNyam Aha | idam eva
   samyag-jñānaṃ sākṣān mokṣa-prāpti-sādhanaṃ na tu dhyānaṃ	samyak--jQAnam sAkzAt mokza--prApti-sADanam na tu DyAnam
   tasyājñānānivartakatvāt | tat tv antaḥkaraṇa-śuddhi-dvāredam eva jñānaṃ	tasya-ajQAna-anivartaka-tvAt | tat tu antaHkaraNa--SudDi--dvAra-idam eva jQAnam
   sampādya krameṇa mokṣaṃ janayatīty uktam |	sampAdya krameNa mokzam janayati-iti uktam |
   kīdṛśaṃ jñānaṃ guhyatamaṃ gopanīyatamam atirahasyatvāt | yato	kIdRSam jQAnam guhyatamam gopanIyatamam ati-rahasya-tvAt | yatas-
   vijñāna-sahitaṃ brahmānubhava-paryantam | īdṛśam atirahasyam apy ahaṃ	vijQAna--sahitam brahma-anuBava--paryantam | IdRSam ati-rahasyam api aham
   śiṣya-guṇādhikyād vakṣyāmi tubhyam anasūyave | asūyā guṇeṣu doṣa-dṛṣṭis	Sizya--guNa-ADikyAt vakzyAmi tuByam anasUyave | asUyA guNezu doza-dRzwi-s
   tad-āviṣkaraṇādi-phalā | sarvadāyam ātmaiśvarya-khyāpanenātmānaṃ	tad--AvizkaraNa-Adi-PalA | sarva-dA-ayam Atma-ESvarya--KyApanena-AtmAnam
   praśaṃsati mat-purastād ity evaṃ rūpā tad-rahitāya | anenārjuava-saṃyamāv	praSaMsati mat--purastAt iti evam rUpA tad--rahitAya | anena-Arjua-va--saMyamO=-
   api śiṣya-guṇau vyākhyātau | punaḥ kīdṛśaṃ jñānaṃ yaj jñātvā prāpya	api Sizya--guNO vyAKyAtO | punar kIdRSam jQAnam yat jQAtvA prApya
   mokṣyase sadya eva saṃsāra-bandhanād aśubhāt sarva-duḥkha-hetoḥ ||1||	mokzyase sadyas eva saMsAra-banDanAt aSuBAt sarva--duHKa-hetoH ||1||
   viśvanāthaḥ ---	viSvanATaH ---
   ārādhyatve prabhor dāsair aiśvaryaṃ yad apekṣitam |	ArADya-tve praBoH dAsEH ESvaryam yat apekzitam |
   tat śuddha-bhakter utkarṣaś cocyate navame sphuṭam ||	tat SudDa-BakteH utkarzaH ca-ucyate navame sPuwam ||
   karma-jñāna-yogādibhyaḥ sakāśāt bhakter eve utkarṣaḥ | sā ca bhaktiḥ	karma--jQAna--yoga-AdiByaH sakASAt BakteH eve utkarzaH | sA ca BaktiH
   pradhānībhūtā kevalā ceti saptamāṣṭamayor uktam | tatrāpi kevalāyā	praDAnIBUtA kevalA ca-iti saptama-azwamayoH uktam | tatra-api kevalAyAH-
   atiprabalāyā jñānavad antaḥkaraṇa-śuddhy-ādy-anapekṣinyā bhakteḥ	atiprabalAyAH jQAna-vat antaHkaraNa--SudDi--Adi--anapekzinyA BakteH
   spaṣṭatayā eva sarvotkarṣaḥ | tasyām apekṣitam aiśvaryaṃ ca vaktuṃ navamo	spazwa-tayA eva sarva-utkarzaH | tasyAm apekzitam ESvaryam ca vaktum navamaH-
   'dhyāya ārabhyate | sarva-śāstra-sāra-bhūtasya gītā-śāstrasyāpi madhyam	aDyAyaH AraByate | sarva--SAstra--sAra-BUtasya gItA--SAstrasya-api maDyam
   adhyāya-ṣaṭkam eva sāram | tasyāpi madhyamau navama-daśamāv eva sārāv ity	aDyAya--zawkam eva sAram | tasya-api maDyamO nava-ma-da-SamO eva sArO iti-
   ato 'tra nirūpayiṣyamāṇam arthaṃ stauti idaṃ tv iti tribhiḥ |	atas atra nirUpayizyamANam arTam stOti idam tu iti triBiH |
   dvitīya-tṛtīyādhyāyādiṣu yad uktaṃ mokṣopayogi-jñānaṃ guhyam |	dvitIya-tRtIya-aDyAya-Adizu yat uktam mokza-upayogi--jQAnam guhyam |
   saptamāṣṭamayor mat-prāpty-upayogi-jñānaṃ jñāyate 'nena bhagavat-tattvam	saptama-azwamayoH mat--prApti--upayogi--jQAnam jQAyate anena Bagavat--tattvam
   iti jñānaṃ bhakti-tattvaṃ guhyataram | atra tu	iti jQAnam Bakti--tattvam guhyataram | atra tu
   kevala-śuddha-bhakti-lakṣaṇaṃ jñānaṃ guhyatamaṃ prakarṣeṇaiva tubhyaṃ	kevala--SudDa--Bakti-lakzaNam jQAnam guhyatamam prakarzeNa-eva tuByam
   vakṣyāmi | atra tu jñāna-śabdena bhaktir avaśyaṃ vyākhyeyā, na tu	vakzyAmi | atra tu jQAna--Sabdena BaktiH avaSyam vyAKyeyA, na tu
   prathama-ṣaṭkoktaṃ prasiddhaṃ jñānam | para-śloke 'vyayam anaśvaram iti	praTama-zawka-uktam prasidDam jQAnam | para--Sloke avyayam anaSvaram iti
   viśeṣaṇa-dānād guṇātītatva-lābhād guṇātītā bhaktir eva | na tu jñānam,	viSezaNa--dAnAt guNa-atIta-tva--lABAt guNa-atItA BaktiH eva | na tu jQAnam,
   tasya sāttvikatvāt | aśraddadhānāḥ puruṣā dharmasyāsya ity agrima-śloke	tasya sAttvika-tvAt | aSraddaDAnAH puruzAH Darmasya-asya iti agrima-Sloke
   dharma-śabdenāpi bhaktir evocyate | anasūyave 'matsarāyety anyo 'pīdam	Darma--Sabdena-api BaktiH eva-ucyate | anasUyave amatsarAya-iti anyaH api-idam
   amatsarāyaivopadiśed iti vidhir vyañjitaḥ | vijñāna-sahitaṃ	amatsarAya-eva-upadiSet iti viDiH vyaQjitaH | vijQAna--sahitam
   mad-aparokṣānubhava-paryantam ity arthaḥ | aśubhāt saṃsārād	mad--aparokza-anuBava--paryantam iti arTaH | aSuBAt saMsArAt-
   bhakti-pratibandhakād antarāyād vā ||1||	Bakti-pratibanDakAt antarAyAt vA ||1||
   baladevaḥ -	baladevaH -

   śuddha-bhakti-sulabha iti saptamādibhyām abhidhāyedānīṃ bhakter uddīpakaṃ	SudDa--Bakti--sulaBaH iti saptama-AdiByAm aBiDAya-idAnIm BakteH uddIpakam
   nijaiśvaryaṃ tasyāḥ prabhāva`acābhidhāsyann ādau tāṃ stauti idam iti	nija-ESvaryam tasyAH praBAva-`acA-aBiDA-asyan AdO tAm stOti idam iti
   tribhiḥ | idaṃ jñānaṃ mat-kīrtanādi-lakṣaṇa-bhakti-rūpam | paratra	triBiH | idam jQAnam mat--kIrtana-Adi--lakzaNa--Bakti--rUpam | paratra

   iti nirukteś ca | tat kila guhyatamam | dvitīyādāv upadiṣṭaṃ	iti nirukteH ca | tat kila guhyatamam | dvitIya-AdO upadizwam
   mad-aiśvarya-jñānaṃ guhyataram ity arthaḥ | navamādāv upadeśyaṃ tu	mad--ESvarya--jQAnam guhyataram iti arTaH | navamAdO upadeSyam tu
   kevala-bhakti-lakṣaṇam idaṃ jñānaṃ guhyatamam ity arthaḥ | tac ca	kevala--Bakti--lakzaNam idam jQAnam guhyatamam iti arTaH | tat ca
   vijñāna-sahitaṃ mad-anubhavāvasānaṃ te vakṣyāmi | kīdṛśāyety āha anasūyava	vijQAna--sahitam mad--anuBava-avasAnam te vakzyAmi | kIdRSAya-iti Aha anasUyava
   iti | mad-guṇeṣu doṣāropa-rahitāya durgamasya	iti | mad-guNezu doza-Ara-upa--rahitAya durgamasya
   sva-rahasyasyānukampayopadeṣṭari mayi nijaiśvarya-prakhyāpanenātmānaṃ	sva-rahasyasya-anukampayA-upadezwari mayi nija-ESvarya--praKyApanena-AtmAnam
   praśaṃsasīti doṣa-dṛṣṭi-śūnyāyety arthaḥ | tenānyo 'py etad anasūyaṃ prati	praSaMsasi-iti doza--dRzwi--SUnyAya-iti arTaH | tena-anyaH api etat anasUyam prati
   brūyād iti darśitam | yaj jñātvā tvam aśubhāt saṃsārān mokṣyase ||1||	brUyAt iti darSitam | yat jQAtvA tvam aSuBAt saMsArAt mokzyase ||1||
   BhG 9.2	Bhu 9.2
   rāja-vidyā rāja-guhyaṃ pavitram idam uttamam |	rAja-vidyA rAja--guhyam pavitram idam uttamam |
   pratyakṣāvagamaṃ dharmyaṃ susukhaṃ kartum avyayam ||2||	pratyakza-avagamam Darmyam su-suKam kartum avyayam ||2||
   śrīdharaḥ - kiṃ ca rājavidyeti | idaṃ jñānaṃ rāja-vidyā vidyānāṃ rājā |	SrIDaraH  kim ca rAja-vidyA-iti | idam jQAnam rAja-vidyA vidyAnAm rAjA |
   rāja-guhyaṃ guhyānāṃ ca rājā | vidyāsu gopyeṣu ca atirahasyaṃ śreṣṭham ity	rAja--guhyam guhyAnAm ca rAjA | vidyAsu gopyezu ca ati-rahasyam SrezWam iti-
   arthaḥ | rāja-dantāditvād upasarjanasya paratvam | rājñāṃ vidyā rājñāṃ	arTaH | rAja--danta-Adi-tvAt upasarjanasya paratvam | rAjQAm vidyA rAjQAm
   guhyam iti vā | uttamaṃ pavitram idam atyanta-pāvanam | jñānināṃ	guhyam iti vA | uttamam pavitram idam atyanta--pAvanam | jQAninAm
   pratyakṣāvagamaṃ ca | pratyakṣaḥ spaṣṭo 'vagamo 'vabodho yasya tat	pratyakza-avagamam ca | pratyakzaH spazwaH avagamaH avaboDaH yasya tat-
   pratyakṣāvagamam | dṛṣṭa-phalam ity arthaḥ | dharmyaṃ dharmād anapetam |	pratyakza-avagamam | dRzwa-Palam iti arTaH | Darmyam DarmAt anapetam |
   vedokta-sarva-dharma-phalatvāt | kartuṃ ca susukhaṃ kartuṃ śakyam ity	veda-ukta--sarva--Darma--Pala-tvAt | kartum ca su-suKam kartum Sakyam iti-
   arthaḥ | avyayaṃ cākṣaya-phalatvāt ||2||	arTaH | avyayam ca-akzaya-Pala-tvAt ||2||
   madhusūdanaḥ - punas tadābhimukhyāya taj-jñānaṃ stauti rājeti | rāja-vidyā	maDusUdanaH  punar tadA-aBimuKyAya taj-jQAnam stOti rAjA-iti | rAja-vidyA
   sarvāsāṃ vidyānāṃ rājā sarvāvidyānāśakatvāt |	sarvAsAm vidyAnAm rAjA sarva-avidyA-nASaka-tvAt |
   vidyāntarasyāvidyaika-deśa-virodhitvāt | tathā rāja-guhyaṃ sarveṣāṃ	vidyA-antarasya-avidyA-eka--deSa--viroDi-tvAt | taTA rAja--guhyam sarvezAm
   guhyānāṃ rājā | aneka-janma-kṛta-sukṛta-sādhyatvena bahubhir ajñātatvāt |	guhyAnAm rAjA | aneka--janma-kRta--su-kRta--sADya-tvena bahuBiH ajQAta-tvAt |
   rāja-dantāditvād upasarjanasya para-nipātaḥ | pavitram idam uttamaṃ	rAja--danta-Adi-tvAt upasarjanasya para--nipAtaH | pavitram idam uttamam
   prāyaścittair hi kiṃcid ekam eva pāpaṃ nivartyate | nivṛttaṃ ca	prAyaScittEH hi kiMcid ekam eva pApam nivartyate | nivRttam ca
   tat-sva-kāraṇe sūkṣma-rūpeṇa tiṣṭhaty eva | yataḥ punas tat-pāpam	tat-sva-kAraNe sUkzma---rUpeNa tizWati eva | yatas punar tat-pApam
   upacinoti puruṣaḥ | idaṃ tv aneka-janma-sahasra-sañcitānāṃ sarveṣām api	upacinoti puruzaH | idam tu aneka--janma--sahasra--saQcitAnAm sarvezAm api
   pāpānāṃ sthūla-sūkṣmāvasthānāṃ tat-kāraṇasya cājñānasya ca sadya	pApAnAm sTUla--sUkzma-avasTAnAm tat-kAraNasya ca-ajQAnasya ca sadyas-
   evocchedakam | ataḥ sarvottamaṃ pāvanam idam eva |	eva-ucCedakam | atas sarva-uttamam pAvanam idam eva |
   na cātīndriye dharma ivātra kasyacit sandehaḥ svarūpataḥ phalataś ca	na ca-atIndriye DarmaH iva-atra kasyacid sandehaH svarUpataH Palatas ca
   pratyakṣatād ity āha pratyakṣāvagamam avagamyate,nenety avagamo mānam	pratyakzatAt iti Aha pratyakza-avagamam avagamyate,nena-iti avagamaH mAnam
   avagamyate prāpyata ity avagamaḥ phalaṃ pratyakṣāvagamo mānam asminn iti	avagamyate prApyate iti avagamaH Palam pratyakza-avagamaH mAnam asmin iti
   svarūpataḥ sākṣi-pratyakṣatvam | pratyakṣo 'vagamo 'syeti phalataḥ	svarUpataH sAkzi--pratyakza-tvam | pratyakzaH avagamaH asya-iti PalataH
   sākṣi-pratyakṣatvam | mayedaṃ viditvam ato naṣṭam idānīm atra mamājñānam	sAkzi--pratyakza-tvam | mayA-idam viditvam atas nazwam idAnIm atra mama-ajQAnam
   iti hi sārvalaukikaḥ sākṣy-anubhavaḥ |	iti hi sArvalOkikaH sAkzi--anuBavaH |
   evaṃ lokānubhava-siddhatve 'pi taj-jñānaṃ dharmyaṃ dharmād anapetam	evam loka-anuBava--sidDa-tve api taj-jQAnam Darmyam DarmAt anapetam
   aneka-janma-saṃcita-niṣkāma-dharma-phalam | tarhi duḥsampādaṃ syān nety	aneka--janma--saMcita--nizkAma--Darma--Palam | tarhi duHsampAdam syAt na-iti-
   āha | susukhaṃ kartuṃ gurūpadarśita-vicāra-sahakṛtena vedānta-vākyena	Aha | su-suKam kartum guru-upadarSita--vicAra--saha-kRtena vedAnta--vAkyena
   sukhena kartuṃ śakyaṃ na deśa-kālādi-vyavadhānam apekṣate	suKena kartum Sakyam na deSa--kAla-Adi--vyavaDAnam apekzate
